<h3
id="ymusic-artist-bio-title">Biography</h3>








<p
id="artistPgBio">The
best-selling
female
performer
of
the
1990s,
Mariah
Carey
rose
to
superstardom
on
the
strength
of
her
stunning
five-octave
voice;
an
elastic
talent
who
moved
easily
from
glossy
ballads
to
hip-hop-inspired
dance-pop,
she
earn...</p>
